109892649923939978960< /UserId.>
<Name>B. June Speaker</Name><Date>1502568457678<//Date><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
I have long been of fan of Stamper Family Optometry and now more than ever. I'm so happy I found Dr. David of the Stamper Clan. ( Three generations of eye docs in this office since 1913. ) After wearing hard contact lenses since age twelve other doctors told me I'd never be able to wear soft lenses. Dr. David, as opposed to his Uncle, Dr. Bruce (called by their first names to avoid the confusion of having two Doctor Stampers in the same office, ) suggested I take a lens holiday. After six months of only wearing glasses I returned and Dr. David was surprised but excited that my corneas looked nearly normal. Decades of polymer plastic lenses do tend to reshape the eye. Mine bounced back like memory foam! Next we discussed my options. Bi-focal glasses? No. Contacts and reading glasses?  No. What about monocular vision? I dunno. He explained and said it wasn't for everyone but I said I was willing to give it a try.

First he determined my dominate eye. This is the eye you use when looking through the viewfinder on a camera or a rifle for that matter. It usually corresponds to your dexterity. He then fitted my dominant left eye for distance vision. Then my right eye was fitted for close-up. He said some people know within an hour if they can do it or not. I was required to stay on the premises for an hour in the event I was one of those people who get nauseous or dizzy. I must say at first the concept alone almost made me cross-eyed but now I think of it as the Poor Man's Lasik Surgery. I could read the clock on a building a block away, I could read the tiny print in a text message and was relieved I didn't have to fumble about for my "reading glasses" to wear over my contacts like I had been doing for way too long.

I was hooked in the first fifteen minutes. No integration issues for my brain!  I don't miss seeing things in stereo, in fact my sight seems to be the best it's ever been and the contacts feel like a dream compared to the old school blind child hard lenses I endured for decades. Dr. David s a great find, he specializes in the "hard to fit" eye. The multi-lingual staff is another big plus. Jhosy got me up to speed on soft lens insertion and removal including a special tip for us "long-nailed" girls. Sweet Esmerelda gave me the visual  test; while Jose was busy tightening my sunglasses that were slipping down my nose but took it a step further and replaced the screw! Sixteen employees, some there ten to twenty years, multi-tasking with the synchronicity of a Swiss watch in their daily routine. The customer service and commitment to the patient's satisfaction is outstanding!</review>

Orbitz reviewer<//Name>
< Review>
I had booked a king bed room on Orbitz for our stay however upon checking in to the motel, we were given a room with 2 double beds as no king bed rooms were available. The room was superbly clean, but keep in mind, this is an OLD motel and it is very close to I-5. The staff is pleasant but there is smoking available outside the rooms and we had people on either side of us sitting at the tiny table and chairs outside their room smoking, so anytime we go in or out of our room, were going through a wall of cigarette smoke. Mind you, these arent complaints or opinions, just facts that visitors should know about before booking the motel. The aviary was neat to see - quite a few small, colorful parrots and a number of cockatiels flying and squawking helped drown out the I-5 noise. The birds are mostly quiet after dark, but they do start their noise early in the morning. We were in the room on the opposite side of where the birds were and we could hear em probably around 6 AM. An you cant really hear I-5 noise, save for a rumbling semi trucks here and there. That being said, Dunsmuir is a beautiful, quiet, off the beaten path town and for a reasonable, not too loud, older motel, Cedar Lodge Motel is just fine. There is a hikable waterfall within a short walk from the motel, and it was a great option for visiting Mount Shasta. Its not too far of a drive to see Shasta and you save a TON of $$$ by not staying in the area of Mount Shasta. Its a better option in the area.</Review>

< text>
Wonderful staff. Extremely accommodating and hospitable. I stayed with my 2 dogs and they were very friendly and happy to have us with them. Great parking. The outdoor grills and picnic area is nice.  They have an aviary with some very neat birds which is novel (no, they don't squawk and keep you awake). A very laid back attitude which I enjoyed greatly.

_________edited after checkout_____

On the day of checkout there was an older woman who seemed to be the owner around. The positive and friendly vibe flipped completely on its head. Instead of being a welcoming and accommodating stay it felt more like we were unwanted and being rushed out. We were the only 3 guests staying at the time and we were told that we could not use the ice machine because the other guests would need ice. She had a worker blowing leaves and dirt at us while we loaded up our trucks with out luggage in an effort to hurry us out.  While we were finishing loading the woman who I assume is the maid came. We had already checked out of one room and got the luxury of watching them clean the other one. It took them maybe 5 minutes to do the whole thing. Basically the changed the sheets and replaced the toilet paper. :/

Vince was the only pleasant employee and if it was just him we dealt with I would have had a much better experience.</text>

<rate>5< /rate>< Review>
Quaint and quiet motel.  We were near some other motels closer to Mt Shasta city and mountain and you can hear the train.  At this motel,  you'd have to be outside and still not be able to hear the train over a parked electric car. They are a dog friendly motel. The whole area is shaded by large trees which was a welcome relief when we arrived and it was over 100¬∞F outside.  Oh,  almost forgot,  the rooms were very clean.  Even though it seems half of the people staying there had dogs,  no animal smell whatsoever in the rooms.  Not a single dog hair when we arrived. I was amazed.  I have a mild animal allergy. I can't sit on a couch a dog or cat uses and i didn't even get a nose tickle.  Whatever they do,  they clean very well.
In closing,  we enjoyed our stay and will definitely stay here again.  There were minor issues like (being a journeyman carpenter) the door to our room rubbed the frame slightly.  But that isn't things i haven't seen elsewhere and it wasn't bad. i have spent more at other hotels and have had to fix doors myself. So the minor issues are specific to my field of expertise and no one else in my party noticed. So,  again,  we'll definitely be staying here again. No pool but no train either.  That train is loud at some other places closer to the tracks.<//Review>

Every staff member was very nice and inclusive with every aspect of my visit. The office is very clean and modern looking. The amenities to take your mind off of dental work, such as hundreds of movies, iPod music, or even a massaging chair were offered to me in a leather binder, much like a menu at a fine restaurant.
Obviously that wouldn't mean a thing if Dr. Muradian's work wasn't up to par. I can assure you he is a very skilled Doctor with a demeanor like you were talking to your favorite relative.
